/*
Created by gabor Horvath 2024.01.29
*/



CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[mfn_tob_getRovidNev]
(
	@KeresesikerelemID int
)
RETURNS VARCHAR(50)
AS
BEGIN
	return (SELECT UPPER(RovidNev) FROM msk_Company c, orn_szi_Company oc , dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk
 WHERE kk.idceg=oc.AllasVallalatKod AND oc.Vallalatkod=c.bukrs AND kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KeresesikerelemID)

END
/*
TEST:
select [dbo].[mfn_tob_getRovidNev](469)
*/

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Najdanovszki Krisztián>
-- Create date: 2020.01.24
-- Description:	
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[msk_tob_fn_elem_readonly] (@ElemNeve VARCHAR(200), @UserID INT, @KKID INT, @AHID INT, @Statusz INT)
RETURNS BIT
AS BEGIN
	DECLARE @Result BIT
	
	SET @Result = 'true'
	
	IF @ElemNeve = 'Toborzasi_folyamatgazda'
		BEGIN
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
			BEGIN
				SET @Result = 'false'
			END
		END

	IF @ElemNeve = 'Toborzo'
		BEGIN
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOB')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
			BEGIN
				SET @Result = 'false'
			END
		END

	IF @ElemNeve = 'Statusz'
		BEGIN
			IF @Statusz = 20 OR @Statusz = ''	/*Terv*/
			 BEGIN
				IF @UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
												LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
												LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
											WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
													AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
					BEGIN
						SET @Result = 'false'
					END
			 END

			IF @Statusz = 25	/*Elküldött*/ 
			 BEGIN
				IF --@UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					--OR 
					@UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
												LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
												LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
											WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_TOBENG')
													AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
					BEGIN
						SET @Result = 'false'
					END
			 END

			IF @Statusz = 21	/*Engedélyezett*/ 
			 BEGIN
				IF --@UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					--OR 
					@UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
												LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
												LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
											WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
													AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
					BEGIN
						SET @Result = 'false'
					END
			 END

			IF @Statusz = 22	/*Publikált*/ 
			 BEGIN
				IF @UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					--OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
					OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
												LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
												LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
											WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
													pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
													AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)
					BEGIN
						SET @Result = 'false'
					END
			 END

			--IF @Statusz = 23	/*Lejárt*/ 
			-- BEGIN
			--	IF @UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
			--		OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
			--		OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
			--									LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
			--									LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
			--								WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
			--										AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)
			--		BEGIN
			--			SET @Result = 'false'
			--		END
			-- END

			--IF @Statusz = 24	/*Lezárt*/ 
			-- BEGIN
			--	IF @UserID IN (SELECT Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
			--		OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = @KKID)
			--		OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
			--									LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
			--									LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
			--								WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
			--										pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
			--										AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0)
			--		BEGIN
			--			SET @Result = 'false'
			--		END
			-- END
		END

	IF @ElemNeve = 'ITadmin'
		BEGIN
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA') 
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
			BEGIN
				SET @Result = 'false'
			END
		END

	IF @ElemNeve = 'HOPadmin'
		BEGIN
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA') 
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
			BEGIN
				SET @Result = 'false'
			END
		END

	RETURN @Result
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Functions\msk_tob_fn_menu_lathatosag.sql =====

-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Najdanovszki Krisztián>
-- Create date: <Create Date, ,>
-- Description:	<Description, ,>
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[msk_tob_fn_menu_lathatosag] (@MMName VARCHAR(200), @UserID INT, @AllasID INT)
RETURNS BIT
AS BEGIN
	DECLARE @Result BIT
	
	SET @Result = 'false'
	
	IF @MMName = 'MMMSKKEXKarrierExcel'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOB' 
											--OR pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXVEZ'
											)
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
						--OR @UserID IN (SELECT idmunkaltato FROM msk_kex_allasajanlatok where Deleted = 0)
						OR @UserID IN (SELECT idvezeto FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetok where Deleted = 0)
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'MMMSKTOB'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOB' 
											--OR pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXVEZ'
											)
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
						OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Deleted = 0)
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'MMMSKTOBEng'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' 
											--OR pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' 
											--OR pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOB' 
											--OR pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXVEZ'
											)
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
						OR @UserID IN (SELECT Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem where Deleted = 0)
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'ScreenMSKKEXKodszotar'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'ToborzasiFolyg'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'Toborzo' AND @AllasID <> 0
			IF @UserID IN (SELECT idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE Deleted=0 AND msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@AllasID)
			OR @UserID IN (SELECT idtoborzo2 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE Deleted=0 AND msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@AllasID)
			OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'Toborzo' AND @AllasID = 0
			IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOB')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'

	IF @MMName = 'Vezeto'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT idvezeto FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetok where Deleted = 0 AND Idallasajanlat=@AllasID)
			OR @UserID IN (SELECT idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE Deleted=0 AND msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@AllasID)
			OR @UserID IN (SELECT idtoborzo2 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE Deleted=0 AND msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@AllasID)
			OR @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_HOPA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'


	IF @MMName = 'IT_admin'
		IF @UserID IN (SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
									WHERE	(pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_ITA' OR
											pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_UITA')
											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND dbo.msk_aktivPeopleID(p.PeopleID)='true')
				SET @Result = 'true'

	RETURN @Result
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Functions\msk_tob_getKeptarDocID.sql =====




-- =============================================
-- Author:		Najdanpvszki Krisztián
-- Create date: 2021-11-29
-- Description:	DocumentID alapján visszaadja a dokumentum elérési útvonalát.
-- =============================================
CREATE FUNCTION [dbo].[msk_tob_getKeptarDocID]
(
	@keptarID INT
)
RETURNS INT
AS 
BEGIN
	DECLARE @res INT = (SELECT DocumentID FROM dbo.msk_tob_keptar WHERE Msk_tob_keptarID=@keptarID)
		
	RETURN @res
END;

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Functions\msk_tob_getma.sql =====

-- =============================================
-- Author:		Horváth Gábor
-- Create date: 2024.01.29.
-- Description:	tob-ban a GETDATE helyett használandó
-- =============================================
CREATE function [dbo].[msk_tob_getma] (
)
RETURNS datetime
AS BEGIN
	declare @dt datetime = dbo.msk_tob_getSetup('GETMA')
	if @dt is null or @dt<'1910-01-01' return getdate()
	declare @ma datetime
	set @ma = @dt;declare @t datetime = CONVERT (time, GETDATE())  ;set @ma = @ma + @t	--TEST ONLY 
	return @ma;
END

/* .........................................
TEST 
Az alábbi részlet beállítja konkrét dátumra majd vissza az aktuálisra a dátumot.
Az idõpont részlet mindig a napi aktuális idõt mutatja csak a dátum áll át

EXEC dbo.msk_tob_setma '2022-12-12 12:12'
SELECT dbo.msk_tob_getma()
EXEC dbo.msk_tob_setma null
SELECT dbo.msk_tob_getma()

*/

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Functions\msk_tob_getSetup.sql =====

-- =============================================
-- Author:		Horváth Gábor
-- Create date: 2024.01.29
-- Description:	TOB ApplicationSetup
-- =============================================
CREATE  function [dbo].[msk_tob_getSetup] (@Code VARCHAR(1000)
)
RETURNS VARCHAR(1000)
AS BEGIN
	DECLARE @res VARCHAR(1000) = (SELECT TOP 1 CodeValue FROM dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup WHERE Code=CONCAT('TOB_',@Code) AND Deleted=0)	
	RETURN @res
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_AdHoc_email_kuldes.sql =====

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_AdHoc_email_kuldes] @AllashID INT, @ElsoAlkalom BIT, @SessionUserID INT
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET ANSI_WARNINGS OFF

	DECLARE @Cimzettek TABLE (Cimzett INT)

	DECLARE @Statusz INT
		SET @Statusz = (SELECT TOP 1 StatuszID FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllashID)

	DECLARE @KKID INT
		SET	@KKID = (SELECT TOP 1 Idkeresesikerelem FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = @AllashID)
	DECLARE @KKName VARCHAR(200)
		SET	@KKName = (SELECT TOP 1 Cim FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)
	DECLARE @Toborzo1 INT = (SELECT TOP 1 Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)
	DECLARE @Toborzo1Neve VARCHAR(1000) = (SELECT TOP 1 Name FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@Toborzo1)

	DECLARE @Letrehozo_vallalat INT
		SET @Letrehozo_vallalat = (SELECT TOP 1 c.VallalatKod FROM dbo.orn_SZI_Company c LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Idceg=c.AllasVallalatKod WHERE kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@KKID)
	DECLARE @Letrehozo_vallalatID INT
		SET @Letrehozo_vallalatID = (SELECT TOP 1 CompanyID FROM dbo.orn_SZI_Company WHERE VallalatKod=@Letrehozo_vallalat)
	DECLARE @Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev VARCHAR(40)
		SET @Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev = (SELECT TOP 1 RovidNev FROM dbo.msk_Company WHERE BUKRS=@Letrehozo_vallalat)
	DECLARE @TemplateID INT
	SET @TemplateID = (SELECT top 1 EmailTemplateSampleID FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE technical_name=CONCAT('tob_',@Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev,'_eng_mod') AND Deleted=0  AND CompanyID=@Letrehozo_vallalatID)

	DECLARE @tmp_Targy  VARCHAR(150) 
		SET @tmp_Targy = (SELECT top 1 EmailSubject FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)
		SET @tmp_Targy = REPLACE(@tmp_Targy, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
	DECLARE @tmp_Szoveg_eredeti  VARCHAR(MAX) 
		SET @tmp_Szoveg_eredeti = (SELECT top 1 EmailBody FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)

	DECLARE @SentToJelentkezoTablaID INT = 0

	DECLARE @base_url VARCHAR(8000) = (SELECT TOP 1 CodeValue FROM dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup WHERE Code='BaseURL' AND Deleted=0)
	DECLARE @url VARCHAR(8000) = '%base%MMMSKTOBToborzas/ScreenMSKTOBKeresesiKerelem'
	SET @url = REPLACE(@url, '%base%', ISNULL(@base_url, ''))

	IF @Statusz = 21
		INSERT INTO @Cimzettek SELECT kk.Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=ah.Idkeresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllashID

	IF @Statusz = 22 --Toborzó, engedélyezõ, folyamatgazda
		BEGIN
		INSERT INTO @Cimzettek SELECT kk.Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=ah.Idkeresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllashID
		--INSERT INTO @Cimzettek SELECT kk.Idengedelyezo FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=ah.Idkeresesikerelem WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllashID
		--INSERT INTO @Cimzettek SELECT p.PeopleID FROM People p 
		--										LEFT JOIN PeopleGroupsPeople pgp ON p.PeopleID = pgp.PeopleID
		--										LEFT JOIN People pp ON pgp.GroupID = pp.PeopleID
		--									WHERE pp.TechnicalName = 'Group_KEXTOBF'
		--											AND pgp.Deleted = 0 AND pp.Deleted = 0 AND p.Deleted = 0 AND p.BUKRS=@Letrehozo_vallalat
		END
		SET @TemplateID = (SELECT top 1 EmailTemplateSampleID FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE technical_name=CONCAT('tob_',@Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev,'_engedelyezett') AND Deleted=0  AND CompanyID=@Letrehozo_vallalatID)

	DECLARE @MailSendLogID INT
	DECLARE @MyCursor CURSOR
	DECLARE @CimzettID INT
	DECLARE @Cimzett_neve VARCHAR(200)
	DECLARE @Cimzett_email VARCHAR(200)
	DECLARE @tmp_Szoveg VARCHAR(MAX)
		BEGIN
			SET @MyCursor = CURSOR FOR
			select Cimzett from @Cimzettek

				OPEN @MyCursor 
				FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor 
				INTO @CimzettID

				WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
				BEGIN
						SET @Cimzett_neve = (SELECT top 1 Name FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@CimzettID)
						SET @Cimzett_email = (SELECT top 1 Email FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@CimzettID)
						DECLARE @Letrehozo_alairas VARCHAR(8000)
						SET @Letrehozo_alairas = (SELECT TOP 1 Alairas
												FROM dbo.msk_kex_emailalairas
												WHERE PeopleID=@Toborzo1 AND Deleted=0)
						
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = @tmp_Szoveg_eredeti
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%cimzett%', ISNULL(@Cimzett_neve, 'Címzett'))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%link%', ISNULL(@url, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%kuldo%', ISNULL(@Toborzo1Neve, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%kuldo_alairas%', ISNULL(@Letrehozo_alairas, ''))

						INSERT INTO dbo.msk_MailSend_Log
						(
							Modul,
							Recipients,
							CopyRecipients,
							BlindCopyRecipients,
							Subject,
							Body,
							BodyFormat,
							Importance,
							FileAttachments,
							MailItemID,
							Created,
							Success,
							Deleted,
							EmailTemplateID,
							CreatedBy,
							SentToJelentkezoID,
							SentToJelentkezoTablaID
						)
						VALUES
						(   'TOB',        -- Modul - varchar(50)
							@Cimzett_email,        -- Recipients - varchar(260)
							NULL,        -- CopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
							NULL,        -- BlindCopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
							@tmp_Targy,        -- Subject - varchar(200)
							@tmp_Szoveg,        -- Body - varchar(max)
							'HTML',        -- BodyFormat - varchar(20)
							'Normal',        -- Importance - varchar(100)
							'',        -- FileAttachments - varchar(8000)
							0,         -- MailItemID - int
							GETDATE(), -- Created - datetime
							0,      -- Success - bit
							0,         -- Deleted - tinyint
							@TemplateID,         -- EmailTemplateID - int
							@SessionUserID,         -- CreatedBy - int
							@CimzettID,         -- SentToJelentkezoID - int
							0          -- SentToJelentkezoTablaID - tinyint
							)

							SET @MailSendLogID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

							EXEC [dbo].[msk_SendMail_dll] 	
									@Modul = 'TOB',
									@Recipients = @Cimzett_email,
									@CopyRecipients  = '',
									@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
									@Subject = @tmp_Targy,
									@Body = @tmp_Szoveg,
									@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
									@Importance = 'Normal',
									@FileAttachments = NULL,
									@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
									@CreatedBy = @SessionUserID,
									@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
									@CimzettTablaID = @SentToJelentkezoTablaID,
									@MailSendLogID = @MailSendLogID

						--exec [dbo].[msk_SendMail]
						--		@Modul = 'TOB',
						--		@Recipients = @Cimzett_email,
						--		@CopyRecipients  = '',
						--		@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
						--		@Subject = @tmp_Targy,
						--		@Body = @tmp_Szoveg,
						--		@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
						--		@Importance = 'Normal',
						--		@FileAttachments = NULL,
						--		@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
						--		@CreatedBy = 1,
						--		@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
						--		@CimzettTablaID = @SentToJelentkezoTablaID

					
				  FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor
				  INTO @CimzettID
				END; 

				CLOSE @MyCursor;
				DEALLOCATE @MyCursor;
			END;
	IF @Statusz = 22 AND @ElsoAlkalom = 1 --MJGY, vezetõ
		BEGIN
			DECLARE @Cimzettek_vezetok TABLE (Cimzett INT, Statuszolo TINYINT, Mjgy INT)
			INSERT INTO @Cimzettek_vezetok (Cimzett,Statuszolo,Mjgy) SELECT kkv.Idvezeto, kkv.Statuszolovezeto, kkv.Mjgy FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok kkv 
												INNER JOIN dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah ON ah.Idkeresesikerelem=kkv.Idkeresesikerelem
											WHERE  ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllashID AND kkv.Deleted=0
			DECLARE @IsStatuszolo TINYINT
			DECLARE @IsMjgy INT
			SET @TemplateID = ((SELECT TOP 1 EmailTemplateSampleID FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE  technical_name=CONCAT('tob_',@Letrehozo_vallalatRovidNev,'_mjgy') AND Deleted=0 AND CompanyID=@Letrehozo_vallalatID))
			SET @tmp_Szoveg_eredeti = (SELECT top 1 EmailBody FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)
			SET @tmp_Targy = (SELECT top 1 EmailSubject FROM dbo.orn_szi_EmailTemplateSample WHERE EmailTemplateSampleID=@TemplateID)



			SET @MyCursor = CURSOR FOR
			select Cimzett,Statuszolo,Mjgy from @Cimzettek_vezetok

				OPEN @MyCursor 
				FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor 
				INTO @CimzettID,@IsStatuszolo,@IsMjgy

				WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
				BEGIN
						SET @Cimzett_neve = (SELECT top 1 Name FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@CimzettID)
						SET @Cimzett_email = (SELECT top 1 Email FROM dbo.People WHERE PeopleID=@CimzettID)
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = @tmp_Szoveg_eredeti
						SET @tmp_Targy = REPLACE(@tmp_Targy, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%cimzett%', ISNULL(@Cimzett_neve, 'Címzett'))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%allashirdetes_neve%', ISNULL(@KKName, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%link%', ISNULL(@url, ''))
						SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%kuldo%', ISNULL(@Toborzo1Neve, ''))
						IF @IsStatuszolo = 1 SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%statuszolo%', 'státuszoló')
							ELSE SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%statuszolo%', '')
						IF @IsMjgy = 10 SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%vezeto_tipus%', 'munkáltatói jogkör gyakorló')
						IF @IsMjgy = 9 SET @tmp_Szoveg = REPLACE(@tmp_Szoveg, '%vezeto_tipus%', 'vezetõ')

						INSERT INTO dbo.msk_MailSend_Log
						(
							Modul,
							Recipients,
							CopyRecipients,
							BlindCopyRecipients,
							Subject,
							Body,
							BodyFormat,
							Importance,
							FileAttachments,
							MailItemID,
							Created,
							Success,
							Deleted,
							EmailTemplateID,
							CreatedBy,
							SentToJelentkezoID,
							SentToJelentkezoTablaID
						)
						VALUES
						(   'TOB',        -- Modul - varchar(50)
							@Cimzett_email,        -- Recipients - varchar(260)
							NULL,        -- CopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
							NULL,        -- BlindCopyRecipients - varchar(8000)
							@tmp_Targy,        -- Subject - varchar(200)
							@tmp_Szoveg,        -- Body - varchar(max)
							'HTML',        -- BodyFormat - varchar(20)
							'Normal',        -- Importance - varchar(100)
							'',        -- FileAttachments - varchar(8000)
							0,         -- MailItemID - int
							GETDATE(), -- Created - datetime
							0,      -- Success - bit
							0,         -- Deleted - tinyint
							@TemplateID,         -- EmailTemplateID - int
							@SessionUserID,         -- CreatedBy - int
							@CimzettID,         -- SentToJelentkezoID - int
							0          -- SentToJelentkezoTablaID - tinyint
							)

							SET @MailSendLogID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

							EXEC [dbo].[msk_SendMail_dll] 	
									@Modul = 'TOB',
									@Recipients = @Cimzett_email,
									@CopyRecipients  = '',
									@BlindCopyRecipients = NULL,
									@Subject = @tmp_Targy,
									@Body = @tmp_Szoveg,
									@BodyFormat = 'HTML',
									@Importance = 'Normal',
									@FileAttachments = NULL,
									@EmailTemplateID = @TemplateID,
									@CreatedBy = @SessionUserID,
									@CimzettID = @CimzettID,
									@CimzettTablaID = @SentToJelentkezoTablaID,
									@MailSendLogID = @MailSendLogID

					
				  FETCH NEXT FROM @MyCursor
				  INTO @CimzettID,@IsStatuszolo,@IsMjgy
				END; 

				CLOSE @MyCursor;
				DEALLOCATE @MyCursor;
			END;


END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_allashirdetescopy.sql =====


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_allashirdetescopy] @prsID integer	
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	


		  /*LOG*/
	DECLARE @UserID INT
	DECLARE @UserSession TABLE (
			[UserID] INT,
			[UserName] VARCHAR(250),
			[Language] VARCHAR(10)
	)
	INSERT INTO @UserSession EXECUTE [dbo].[osp_getPrsDataFromXml_UserSession] @prsID
	SELECT @UserID = (SELECT TOP 1 [UserID] FROM @UserSession)


	DECLARE @tmp_prs TABLE
	(
	ornAlias Varchar(100),
	ornType Varchar(100),
	ornValue Varchar(100),
	inOut Varchar(100)
	)
	INSERT INTO @tmp_prs execute osp_getPrsDataFromXml_Filters @prsID
	DECLARE @ID INT = (SELECT TOP 1 ornValue FROM @tmp_prs WHERE ornAlias='Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID_ID')


	insert into msk_tob_allashirdetesek ([Idkeresesikerelem]
      ,[Targy]
      ,[StatuszID]
      ,[Datum_lejarat]
      ,[CsatolmanyID]
      ,[Fejlecszoveg]
      ,[Feladatok]
      ,[Tulajdonsagok]
      ,[Elvarasok]
      ,[Elonytjelent]
      ,[Juttatasok]
      ,[Tovabbi_info]
      ,[Toborzo_info]
      ,[Toborzonev]
      ,[Toborzotelefonszam]
      ,[Vallalatibemutatkozo]
      ,[Datum_jovahagyas]
      ,[Datum_publikalas]
      ,[Link]
      ,[Datum_lezaras]
      ,[VegzettsegiszintID]
      ,[Pubcsoportportal]
      ,[PubCVO]
      ,[PubSTA]
      ,[Deleted]
      ,[FenykepURL]
	  ,[VideoURL]
      ,[LetrehozoID])
(select [Idkeresesikerelem]
      ,CONCAT([Targy],'_másolat')
      ,20
      ,[Datum_lejarat]
      ,[CsatolmanyID]
      ,[Fejlecszoveg]
      ,[Feladatok]
      ,[Tulajdonsagok]
      ,[Elvarasok]
      ,[Elonytjelent]
      ,[Juttatasok]
      ,[Tovabbi_info]
      ,[Toborzo_info]
      ,[Toborzonev]
      ,[Toborzotelefonszam]
      ,[Vallalatibemutatkozo]
      ,[Datum_jovahagyas]
      ,[Datum_publikalas]
      ,[Link]
      ,[Datum_lezaras]
      ,[VegzettsegiszintID]
      ,0
      ,0
      ,0
      ,0
      ,[FenykepURL]
	  ,[VideoURL]
      ,@UserID
from msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = @ID)

/*
	declare @sel nvarchar(500)
	set @sel = 'Update Msk_tob_allashirdetesek set PubCVO=''@PubCVO'', PubSTA=''@PubSTA'', Pubcsoportportal=''@Pubcsoportportal'' WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = @ID'

	exec sp_executesql @sel
	*/
	SELECT 'Létrejött az új álláshirdetés szöveg!'

END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_allashirdeteslink.sql =====


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_allashirdeteslink] @allasID INTEGER, @link VARCHAR(2000) 	
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	


	DECLARE @Success BIT

	UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek SET Link=@link ,statuszCSP=1, Datum_publikalas = GETDATE()
	WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@allasID
	
	/* LOG */
	INSERT INTO dbo.msk_log	(name,value,created) VALUES	('Tárolt beírta a LINK-et amit az interfésztõl kapott az álláshot:', @link, SYSDATETIME())
    
	/*Válasz a DLL-nek*/
	SET @Success = 'true'
	SELECT @Success

END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_allashirdetespub.sql =====


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_allashirdetespub] @allasID INTEGER, @PubCSP TINYINT, @PubCVO TINYINT, @PubSTA TINYINT
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	SET ANSI_WARNINGS OFF

	INSERT INTO dbo.msk_log
	(
	    name,
	    value,
	    created
	)
	VALUES
	(   'PubCSP-tároltban',           -- name - varchar(100)
	    @PubCSP,           -- value - varchar(max)
	    SYSDATETIME() -- created - datetime2(7)
	    )

	/* Pipák lementése a formról és státuszátállítás*/
	UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek SET StatuszID=22, Pubcsoportportal=@PubCSP, PubCVO=@PubCVO, PubSTA=@PubSTA
	WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@allasID

	DECLARE @Success BIT

      DECLARE @id INT
      DECLARE @company VARCHAR(100)
      DECLARE @title VARCHAR(255)
      DECLARE @description VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @location VARCHAR(250)
      DECLARE @category INT
      DECLARE @companyid INT
      DECLARE @requirements VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @qualities VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @benefits VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @activationDate DATE
      DECLARE @expirationDate DATE
      DECLARE @contract VARCHAR(250)
      DECLARE @vacancyNumber INT
      DECLARE @workLocation VARCHAR(250)
      DECLARE @tasks VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @additionalInfo VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @recruiterInfo VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @recruiterId VARCHAR(10)
      DECLARE @recruiterEmail VARCHAR(100)
      DECLARE @industry VARCHAR(MAX)
      DECLARE @hierarchyLeve VARCHAR(200)
      DECLARE @educationType VARCHAR(250)
      DECLARE @educationField VARCHAR(250)
      DECLARE @Idtoborzo1 INT
      DECLARE @Idtoborzo2 INT
      DECLARE @Engedelyezesidatum DATE
      DECLARE @Iktatoszam VARCHAR(50)
	  DECLARE @FoglalkoztatasifokID INT
	  DECLARE @Link VARCHAR(2000)
	  DECLARE @MAPJob TINYINT
	  DECLARE @Cv TINYINT
	  DECLARE @VideoURL VARCHAR(1000)
	  DECLARE @properties VARCHAR(MAX)

	SELECT
	   @id=[id]
      ,@company=[company]
      ,@title=[title]
      ,@description=[description]
      ,@location=[location]
      ,@category=[category]
      ,@companyid=[companyid]
      ,@requirements=[requirements]
      ,@qualities=[qualities]
      ,@benefits=[benefits]
      ,@activationDate=[activationDate]
      ,@expirationDate=[expirationDate]
      ,@contract=[contract]
      ,@vacancyNumber=[vacancyNumber]
      ,@workLocation=[workLocation]
      ,@tasks=[tasks]
      ,@additionalInfo=[additionalInfo]
      ,@recruiterInfo=[recruiterInfo]
      ,@recruiterId=[recruiterId]
      ,@recruiterEmail=[recruiterEmail]
      ,@industry=[industry]
      ,@hierarchyLeve=[hierarchyLeve]
      ,@educationType=[educationType]
      ,@educationField=[educationField]
      ,@Idtoborzo1=[Idtoborzo1]
      ,@Idtoborzo2=[Idtoborzo2]
      ,@Engedelyezesidatum=[Engedelyezesidatum]
      ,@Iktatoszam=[Iktatoszam]
	  ,@FoglalkoztatasifokID=[schedule]
	  ,@Link=[Link]
	  ,@MAPJob=MAPJob
	  ,@Cv=Cv
	  ,@VideoURL=recruiterFelvado
	  ,@properties=properties
	  FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_portalallashirdetes]
	  WHERE id=@allasID

	  IF EXISTS(SELECT * FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@allasID)
		  BEGIN
			UPDATE dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok 
				SET 
					targy=@title,
					leiras=@description,
					hely=@location,
					idkategoria=@category,
					datum_aktivalas=@activationDate,
					datum_lejarat=@expirationDate,
					szerzodes_fajta=@contract,
					foglalkoztatasi_fok=@FoglalkoztatasifokID,
					poziciok_szama=@vacancyNumber,
					munkavegzes_helye=@workLocation,
					feladatok=@tasks,
					elvarasok=@requirements,
					elonytjelent=@qualities,
					juttatasok=@benefits,
					tovabbi_info=@additionalInfo,
					toborzo_info=@recruiterInfo,
					toborzo_torzsszam=@recruiterId,
					igazgatosag=@industry,
					munkakor_csoport=@hierarchyLeve,
					kepzes_fajta=@educationType,
					kepzes_szakirany=@educationField,
					toborzo_email=@recruiterEmail,
					toborzo_felvado=@VideoURL,
					map_job=@MAPJob,
					cv=@Cv,
					engedely_datuma=@Engedelyezesidatum,
					pozicio_szama=@vacancyNumber,
					idceg=@companyid,
					link=@Link,
					idtoborzo1=@Idtoborzo1,
					idtoborzo2=@Idtoborzo2,
					engedely_iktatoszama=@Iktatoszam,
					Tulajdonsagok=@properties
			WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@allasID 	
			
			INSERT INTO dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetok
			(
				Idvezeto,
				Idallasajanlat,
				Mjgy,
				Deleted,
				Statuszolovezeto
			)
			(SELECT kkv.Idvezeto,
				@allasID,
				kkv.Mjgy,
				0,
				kkv.Statuszolovezeto	
				FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=ah.Idkeresesikerelem
													LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok kkv ON kkv.Idkeresesikerelem=kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID
				WHERE ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@allasID AND kkv.Deleted=0
				AND NOT EXISTS(SELECT * FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetok WHERE Idallasajanlat=@allasID AND Idvezeto=kkv.Idvezeto AND Deleted=0))	

			/*E-mail küldések elsõ publikáláskor*/
			EXEC dbo.msk_tob_AdHoc_email_kuldes @allasID, 0, 1
		  END
	  ELSE
		  BEGIN
			IF (SELECT TOP 1 toborzo_feluliras_flag FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@allasID)=1
				BEGIN
					SET @Idtoborzo1=(SELECT TOP 1 @Idtoborzo1 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@allasID)
					SET @Idtoborzo2=(SELECT TOP 1 @Idtoborzo2 FROM dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID=@allasID)
                END
				
			INSERT INTO dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlatok
			(
			    msk_kex_allasajanlatokID,
			    uzletag,
			    targy,
			    leiras,
			    hely,
			    idkategoria,
			    idceg,
			    reszleg,
			    elvarasok,
			    elonytjelent,
			    juttatasok,
			    datum_aktivalas,
			    datum_lejarat,
			    szerzodes_fajta,
			    foglalkoztatasi_fok,
			    poziciok_szama,
			    munkavegzes_helye,
			    feladatok,
			    tovabbi_info,
			    toborzo_info,
			    toborzo_torzsszam,
			    vallalat,
			    igazgatosag,
			    munkakor_csoport,
			    kepzes_fajta,
			    kepzes_szakirany,
			    szak,
			    idegen_nyelv,
			    informatika,
			    szakmai_tapasztalat,
			    jogositvany,
			    link,
			    toborzo_feluliras_flag,
			    idszin,
			    idtoborzo1,
			    idtoborzo2,
			    idvezeto,
			    datum_tanfolyam,
			    idtanfolyamhely,
			    idtanfolyamtipus,
			    datum_lezaras,
			    aktiv,
			    datum_tanfolyam_szoveges,
			    min_tapasztalat,
			    min_vegzettseg,
			    vezetoi_engedely,
			    alt_ceg_nev,
			    alt_email,
			    alt_telefon,
			    ceg_elrejtese,
			    jelentkezes_gomb,
			    idfogado,
			    toborzo_email,
			    toborzo_felvado,
			    map_job,
			    cv,
			    kvalifikacio,
			    engedely_iktatoszama,
			    engedely_datuma,
			    pozicio_szama,
			    Deleted,
			    idmunkaltato,
			    Created,
			    Idlezarasindok,
				Tulajdonsagok
			)
			VALUES
			(   @allasID,         -- msk_kex_allasajanlatokID - int
			    @company,        -- uzletag - varchar(100)
			    @title,        -- targy - varchar(255)
			    @description,        -- leiras - varchar(max)
			    @location,        -- hely - varchar(255)
			    @category,         -- idkategoria - int
			    @companyid,         -- idceg - int
			    NULL,        -- reszleg - varchar(255)
			    @requirements,        -- elvarasok - varchar(max)
			    @qualities,        -- elonytjelent - varchar(max)
			    @benefits,        -- juttatasok - varchar(max)
			    @activationDate, -- datum_aktivalas - date
			    @expirationDate, -- datum_lejarat - date
			    @contract,        -- szerzodes_fajta - varchar(255)
			    @FoglalkoztatasifokID,        -- foglalkoztatasi_fok - varchar(50)
			    @vacancyNumber,         -- poziciok_szama - int
			    @workLocation,        -- munkavegzes_helye - varchar(255)
			    @tasks,        -- feladatok - varchar(max)
			    @additionalInfo,        -- tovabbi_info - varchar(max)
			    @recruiterInfo,        -- toborzo_info - varchar(max)
			    @recruiterId,        -- toborzo_torzsszam - varchar(10)
			    NULL,        -- vallalat - varchar(3)
			    @industry,        -- igazgatosag - varchar(4)
			    @hierarchyLeve,        -- munkakor_csoport - varchar(4)
			    @educationType,        -- kepzes_fajta - varchar(4)
			    @educationField,        -- kepzes_szakirany - varchar(4)
			    NULL,        -- szak - varchar(255)
			    NULL,        -- idegen_nyelv - varchar(max)
			    NULL,        -- informatika - varchar(max)
			    NULL,        -- szakmai_tapasztalat - varchar(max)
			    NULL,        -- jogositvany - varchar(max)
			    @Link,        -- link - varchar(2000)
			    0,         -- toborzo_feluliras_flag - tinyint
			    NULL,         -- idszin - int
			    @Idtoborzo1,         -- idtoborzo1 - int
			    @Idtoborzo2,         -- idtoborzo2 - int
			    0,         -- idvezeto - int
			    NULL, -- datum_tanfolyam - date
			    0,         -- idtanfolyamhely - int
			    0,         -- idtanfolyamtipus - int
			    NULL, -- datum_lezaras - date
			    0,         -- aktiv - tinyint
			    NULL,       -- datum_tanfolyam_szoveges - nchar(7)
			    0,         -- min_tapasztalat - int
			    0,         -- min_vegzettseg - int
			    NULL,      -- vezetoi_engedely - bit
			    NULL,        -- alt_ceg_nev - varchar(50)
			    NULL,        -- alt_email - varchar(50)
			    NULL,        -- alt_telefon - varchar(50)
			    NULL,      -- ceg_elrejtese - bit
			    NULL,      -- jelentkezes_gomb - bit
			    NULL,         -- idfogado - int
			    @recruiterEmail,        -- toborzo_email - varchar(255)
			    @VideoURL,        -- toborzo_felvado - varchar(255)
			    @MAPJob,         -- map_job - int
			    @Cv,         -- cv - int
			    NULL,        -- kvalifikacio - varchar(255)
			    @Iktatoszam,        -- engedely_iktatoszama - varchar(255)
			    @Engedelyezesidatum, -- engedely_datuma - date
			    @vacancyNumber,         -- pozicio_szama - int
			    0,         -- Deleted - tinyint
			    0,         -- idmunkaltato - int
			    GETDATE(), -- Created - datetime
			    NULL,          -- Idlezarasindok - int
				@properties    --Tulajdonsagok varchar(MAX)
 			    )

			INSERT INTO dbo.msk_kex_allasajanlat_vezetok
			(
				Idvezeto,
				Idallasajanlat,
				Mjgy,
				Deleted,
				Statuszolovezeto
			)
			(SELECT kkv.Idvezeto,
				@allasID,
				kkv.Mjgy,
				0,
				kkv.Statuszolovezeto	
				FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem kk ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=ah.Idkeresesikerelem
													LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok kkv ON kkv.Idkeresesikerelem=kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID
				WHERE ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@allasID AND kkv.Deleted=0)

			/*E-mail küldések elsõ publikáláskor*/
			EXEC dbo.msk_tob_AdHoc_email_kuldes @allasID, 1, 1
		  END

    
	/* LOG */
	INSERT INTO dbo.msk_log	(name,value,created) VALUES	('Tárolt bemásolta a KEX-be az állásajánlatot', @allasID, SYSDATETIME())

	/* frissíti az msk_kex_advertlistchangelog táblát */
    EXEC [dbo].[msk_tob_msk_kex_advertlistchangelog_frissites] @allasID

	/*Válasz a DLL-nek*/
	SET @Success = 'true'
	SELECT @Success

END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_CVO_DLL_select.sql =====

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_CVO_DLL_select] 
AS
BEGIN
select (
select PID as "@ID",
ISNULL(case when ltrim(PCOMPANY)='' then '-' else PCOMPANY END,'') as company,
ISNULL(PTITLE,'') as title, 
ISNULL(PDESCRIPTION,'') as description, 
ISNULL(plocation,'') as 'locations/location', 
ISNULL(pcategory,'') as 'categories/category',
ISNULL(PcompanyID,'') as companyID, 
ISNULL(pdepartment,'') as department, 
ISNULL(prequirements,'') as requirements, 
ISNULL(pqualities,'') as qualities, 
ISNULL(pbenefits,'') as benefits, 
ISNULL(pminexperience,'') as min_experience, 
ISNULL(pmineducation,'') as min_education, 
ISNULL(pdriverlicence,'') as driver_license,
ISNULL(plink,'') as link, 
ISNULL(pactivationdate,'') as activation_date, 
ISNULL(pexpirationdate,'') as expiration_date, 
ISNULL(pcontract,'') as contract, 
ISNULL(pschedule,'') as schedule, 
ISNULL(pcompanyname,'') as company_name, 
ISNULL(pemail,'') as email, 
ISNULL(pphone,'') as phone, 
ISNULL(PVACANCYNUMBER,'') as vacancy_nr, 
ISNULL(pworklocation,'') as work_location, 
'false' as hide_company, 
'false' as show_apply_button, 
ISNULL(pcustomtemplateID,'') as custom_template_ID, 
ISNULL(ptasks,'') as tasks, 
ISNULL(padditionalinfo,'') as additional_info, 
ISNULL(precruiterinfo,'') as recruiter_info, 
ISNULL(pfenykepurl,'') as fenykepurl,
ISNULL(pvideourl,'') as videourl,
ISNULL(pproperties,'') as properties
from msk_tob_CVO /* where padditionalinfo is not null and padditionalinfo<>'' */
for xml path('advert'), root('WebAdverts')
) as xml
end

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_CVO_item.sql =====

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_CVO_item] 
@ID int
AS
BEGIN
	update msk_tob_allashirdetesek set StatuszCVO=1 where Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = @ID


	insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('CVO Interfész ITEM OK',@ID,getdate())
	select 'True'
END

@Guid varchar(100) = ''
AS
BEGIN
	insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('CVO Interfész OK',@Guid,getdate())
	select 'True'
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_keresesikerelem_masolas.sql =====

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem_masolas] @ID integer	
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	
	DECLARE @tmp_prs TABLE
	(
		ornAlias Varchar(100),
		ornType Varchar(100),
		ornValue Varchar(100),
		inOut Varchar(100)
	)
	INSERT INTO @tmp_prs execute osp_getPrsDataFromXml_Filters @ID
	DECLARE @idkkmasolas INT = (SELECT TOP 1 ornValue FROM @tmp_prs WHERE ornAlias='Template_MSKTOBKeresesiKerelemMasolas')
	DECLARE @kkID INT = (SELECT TOP 1 ornValue FROM @tmp_prs WHERE ornAlias='Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID_ID')

	DECLARE @tmp_user TABLE(
	UserID INT,UserName VARCHAR(100),Language VARCHAR(100))
	INSERT INTO @tmp_user EXECUTE dbo.osp_getPrsDataFromXml_UserSession @ID
	DECLARE @UserID INT = (SELECT TOP 1 UserID FROM @tmp_user)

	DECLARE @UjKK INT


  IF @idkkmasolas = 1 OR @idkkmasolas = 2
	BEGIN

		  INSERT INTO dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem
		  (
		      Cim,
		      StatuszID,
		      Iktatoszam,
		      Engedelyezesidatum,
		      Munkakor,
		      Lejaratidatum,
		      Pozicioszam,
		      TeruletiigazgatosagID,
		      SzakteruletID,
		      SzervezetiegyesegID,
		      SzerzodesfajtaID,
		      MunkavegzeshelyeID,
		      Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb,
		      Cv,
		      MunkakorcsoportID,
		      FoglalkoztatasifokID,
		      Kepzes_fajtaID,
		      Kepzes_szakiranyID,
		      MMKkod,
		      Berlatszik,
		      Berkotelezo,
		      Map_job,
		      Idtoborzo1,
		      Idtoborzo2,
		      Idengedelyezo,
		      Idceg,
		      Deleted,
		      Szerzodes_befejezes,
		      Lezaras
		  )
		  (SELECT
			   CONCAT([Cim],'_másolat')
			  ,NULL
			  ,[Iktatoszam]
			  ,[Engedelyezesidatum]
			  ,[Munkakor]
			  ,NULL
			  ,[Pozicioszam]
			  ,[TeruletiigazgatosagID]
			  ,[SzakteruletID]
			  ,[SzervezetiegyesegID]
			  ,[SzerzodesfajtaID]
			  ,[MunkavegzeshelyeID]
			  ,[Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb]
			  ,[Cv]
			  ,[MunkakorcsoportID]
			  ,[FoglalkoztatasifokID]
			  ,[Kepzes_fajtaID]
			  ,[Kepzes_szakiranyID]
			  ,[MMKkod]
			  ,[Berlatszik]
			  ,[Berkotelezo]
			  ,[Map_job]
			  ,[Idtoborzo1]
			  ,[Idtoborzo2]
			  ,[Idengedelyezo]
			  ,[Idceg]
			  ,0
			  ,[Szerzodes_befejezes]
			  ,0
			FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem]
			WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@kkID)

		SET @UjKK = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

	END

	IF @idkkmasolas = 1
	BEGIN
		BEGIN TRAN
		DECLARE @msk_tob_allashirdetesek TABLE
			(
			[Idkeresesikerelem] [INT] NULL,
			[Targy] [VARCHAR](255) NULL,
			[StatuszID] [INT] NULL,
			[Datum_lejarat] [DATE] NULL,
			[CsatolmanyID] [INT] NULL,
			[Fejlecszoveg] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Feladatok] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Tulajdonsagok] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Elvarasok] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Elonytjelent] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Juttatasok] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Tovabbi_info] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Toborzo_info] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Toborzonev] [VARCHAR](250) NULL,
			[Toborzotelefonszam] [VARCHAR](50) NULL,
			[Vallalatibemutatkozo] [VARCHAR](MAX) NULL,
			[Datum_jovahagyas] [DATE] NULL,
			[Datum_publikalas] [DATE] NULL,
			[Link] [VARCHAR](2000) NULL,
			[Datum_lezaras] [DATE] NULL,
			[VegzettsegiszintID] [INT] NULL,
			[Pubcsoportportal] [BIT] NULL,
			[PubCVO] [BIT] NULL,
			[PubSTA] [BIT] NULL,
			[FenykepURL] [VARCHAR](1000) NULL,
			[VideoURL] [VARCHAR](1000) NULL,
			[Deleted] [TINYINT] NULL,
			[LetrehozoID] [INT] NULL)

			INSERT INTO @msk_tob_allashirdetesek
			(
				Idkeresesikerelem,
				Targy,
				StatuszID,
				Datum_lejarat,
				CsatolmanyID,
				Fejlecszoveg,
				Feladatok,
				Tulajdonsagok,
				Elvarasok,
				Elonytjelent,
				Juttatasok,
				Tovabbi_info,
				Toborzo_info,
				Toborzonev,
				Toborzotelefonszam,
				Vallalatibemutatkozo,
				Datum_jovahagyas,
				Datum_publikalas,
				Link,
				Datum_lezaras,
				VegzettsegiszintID,
				Pubcsoportportal,
				PubCVO,
				PubSTA,
				Deleted,		
				LetrehozoID,
				FenykepURL,
				VideoURL
			)
			SELECT TOP 1
			   @UjKK AS Idkeresesikerelem
			  ,CONCAT([Targy],'_másolat') AS Targy
			  ,20 AS StatuszID
			  ,NULL AS Datum_lejarat
			  ,[CsatolmanyID]
			  ,[Fejlecszoveg]
			  ,[Feladatok]
			  ,[Tulajdonsagok]
			  ,[Elvarasok]
			  ,[Elonytjelent]
			  ,[Juttatasok]
			  ,[Tovabbi_info]
			  ,[Toborzo_info]
			  ,[Toborzonev]
			  ,[Toborzotelefonszam]
			  ,[Vallalatibemutatkozo]
			  ,NULL AS Datum_jovahagyas
			  ,NULL AS Datum_publikalas
			  ,[Link]
			  ,NULL AS Datum_lezaras
			  ,[VegzettsegiszintID]
			  ,[Pubcsoportportal]
			  ,[PubCVO]
			  ,[PubSTA]
			  ,0 AS Deleted
			  ,@UserID AS LetrehozoID
			  ,FenykepURL
			  ,VideoURL
		  FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_allashirdetesek]
		  WHERE Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID AND Deleted=0
		  ORDER BY Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID DESC

		  INSERT INTO dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek
			(
				Idkeresesikerelem,Targy,StatuszID,Datum_lejarat,CsatolmanyID,Fejlecszoveg,Feladatok,
				Tulajdonsagok,Elvarasok,Elonytjelent,Juttatasok,Tovabbi_info,Toborzo_info,Toborzonev,
				Toborzotelefonszam,Vallalatibemutatkozo,Datum_jovahagyas,Datum_publikalas,Link,Datum_lezaras,
				VegzettsegiszintID,Pubcsoportportal,PubCVO,PubSTA,Deleted,LetrehozoID,FenykepURL,VideoURL)
			(SELECT Idkeresesikerelem,
					Targy,
					StatuszID,
					Datum_lejarat,
					CsatolmanyID,
					Fejlecszoveg,
					Feladatok,
					Tulajdonsagok,
					Elvarasok,
					Elonytjelent,
					Juttatasok,
					Tovabbi_info,
					Toborzo_info,
					Toborzonev,
					Toborzotelefonszam,
					Vallalatibemutatkozo,
					Datum_jovahagyas,
					Datum_publikalas,
					Link,
					Datum_lezaras,
					VegzettsegiszintID,
					Pubcsoportportal,
					PubCVO,
					PubSTA,
					Deleted,
					LetrehozoID,
					FenykepURL,
					VideoURL
			  FROM @msk_tob_allashirdetesek)
		COMMIT
	END
	
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_keresesikerelem_masolas_betoltetlen.sql =====


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem_masolas_betoltetlen] 
	@kkID integer	--keresesikerelemID,
	,@UserID INT
AS 
BEGIN
	DECLARE @UjKK INT
	declare @UJSORSZAM bit = 0 -- 1 esetén új sorszámot generál a másolt adatoknak #86289 

	declare @has int = (select count(*) from msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and StatuszID=32 and Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID )

	if @has = 0 begin
		return
	end

		  INSERT INTO dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem
		  (
		      Cim,
		      StatuszID,
		      Iktatoszam,
		      Engedelyezesidatum,
		      Munkakor,
		      Lejaratidatum,
		      Pozicioszam,
		      TeruletiigazgatosagID,
		      SzakteruletID,
		      SzervezetiegyesegID,
		      SzerzodesfajtaID,
		      MunkavegzeshelyeID,
		      Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb,
		      Cv,
		      MunkakorcsoportID,
		      FoglalkoztatasifokID,
		      Kepzes_fajtaID,
		      Kepzes_szakiranyID,
		      MMKkod,
		      Berlatszik,
		      Berkotelezo,
		      Map_job,
		      Idtoborzo1,
		      Idtoborzo2,
		      Idengedelyezo,
		      Idceg,
		      Deleted,
		      Szerzodes_befejezes,
		      Lezaras
		  )
		  (SELECT
			   CONCAT([Cim],'_másolat')
			  ,NULL
			  ,[Iktatoszam]
			  ,[Engedelyezesidatum]
			  ,[Munkakor]
			  ,NULL
			  ,[Pozicioszam]
			  ,[TeruletiigazgatosagID]
			  ,[SzakteruletID]
			  ,[SzervezetiegyesegID]
			  ,[SzerzodesfajtaID]
			  ,[MunkavegzeshelyeID]
			  ,[Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb]
			  ,[Cv]
			  ,[MunkakorcsoportID]
			  ,[FoglalkoztatasifokID]
			  ,[Kepzes_fajtaID]
			  ,[Kepzes_szakiranyID]
			  ,[MMKkod]
			  ,[Berlatszik]
			  ,[Berkotelezo]
			  ,[Map_job]
			  ,[Idtoborzo1]
			  ,[Idtoborzo2]
			  ,[Idengedelyezo]
			  ,[Idceg]
			  ,0
			  ,[Szerzodes_befejezes]
			  ,0
			FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem]
			WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID=@kkID)

		SET @UjKK = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

		INSERT INTO dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek
		(
		    Idkeresesikerelem,
		    Targy,
		    StatuszID,
		    Datum_lejarat,
		    CsatolmanyID,
		    Fejlecszoveg,
		    Feladatok,
		    Tulajdonsagok,
		    Elvarasok,
		    Elonytjelent,
		    Juttatasok,
		    Tovabbi_info,
		    Toborzo_info,
		    Toborzonev,
		    Toborzotelefonszam,
		    Vallalatibemutatkozo,
		    Datum_jovahagyas,
		    Datum_publikalas,
		    Link,
		    Datum_lezaras,
		    VegzettsegiszintID,
		    Pubcsoportportal,
		    PubCVO,
		    PubSTA,
		    Deleted,
		    LetrehozoID,
			FenykepURL,
			VideoURL
		)
		(SELECT 
			   @UjKK
			  ,CONCAT([Targy],'_másolat')
			  ,20
			  ,NULL
			  ,[CsatolmanyID]
			  ,[Fejlecszoveg]
			  ,[Feladatok]
			  ,[Tulajdonsagok]
			  ,[Elvarasok]
			  ,[Elonytjelent]
			  ,[Juttatasok]
			  ,[Tovabbi_info]
			  ,[Toborzo_info]
			  ,[Toborzonev]
			  ,[Toborzotelefonszam]
			  ,[Vallalatibemutatkozo]
			  ,NULL
			  ,NULL
			  ,[Link]
			  ,NULL
			  ,[VegzettsegiszintID]
			  ,[Pubcsoportportal]
			  ,[PubCVO]
			  ,[PubSTA]
			  ,0
			  ,@UserID
			  ,FenykepURL
			  ,VideoURL
		  FROM [dbo].[msk_tob_allashirdetesek]
		  WHERE Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID AND Deleted=0)
	

	declare
     @VallalatRovidNeve VARCHAR(50) = (select [dbo].[mfn_tob_getRovidNev](@UjKK))
	,@tanfolyamos BIT = (select top 1 case when Poziciotipus=41 then 1 else 0 end from msk_tob_headpozicio where deleted=0 and Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID ) 
    ,@mennyiseg INT = @has
	,@datum date = (select top 1 engedelyezesidatum from msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and StatuszID=32 and Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID order by PozicioID)
	,@PozicioInfo varchar(50)
	,@ikt varchar(max)
	,@Alszam int =0
	,@Stat2 int
	,@ID int = 0		
	,@IDCursor CURSOR

	if @UJSORSZAM=1 begin
		if @tanfolyamos = 1 begin
			EXEC msp_tob_getIktatoszam @UjKK,@VallalatRovidNeve,@tanfolyamos,@mennyiseg,@datum,''
		end
		else begin
			SET @IDCursor = CURSOR FOR select PozicioID from msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and StatuszID=32 and Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID order by pozicioID
			OPEN @IDCursor
			FETCH NEXT FROM @IDCursor INTO @ID
			WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
			BEGIN
				select top 1 @datum=engedelyezesidatum,@PozicioInfo=PozicioInfo from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID=@ID
				EXEC msp_tob_getIktatoszam @UjKK,@VallalatRovidNeve,@tanfolyamos,1,@datum,@PozicioInfo
				FETCH NEXT FROM @IDCursor INTO @ID
			END;
			CLOSE @IDCursor;
			DEALLOCATE @IDCursor;
	
		end
	end else begin
			set @ID = 0		
			SET @IDCursor = CURSOR FOR select PozicioID from msk_tob_pozicio where deleted=0 and StatuszID=32 and Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID order by pozicioID
			OPEN @IDCursor
			FETCH NEXT FROM @IDCursor INTO @ID
			WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
			BEGIN
				select top 1 @Stat2=StatuszID,@ikt=Iktatoszam,@datum=engedelyezesidatum,@PozicioInfo=PozicioInfo from msk_tob_pozicio where PozicioID=@ID
				SET @Alszam = CONVERT(INT, RIGHT(@ikt, 3)) ;

				INSERT INTO msk_tob_pozicio (Idkeresesikerelem, Iktatoszam, Aliktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, StatuszID, Deleted,PozicioInfo)
				VALUES (@UjKK, @ikt, @Alszam, @datum, @Stat2,0,@PozicioInfo);

				FETCH NEXT FROM @IDCursor INTO @ID
			END;
			CLOSE @IDCursor;
			DEALLOCATE @IDCursor;

			INSERT INTO msk_tob_headpozicio (Idkeresesikerelem, Poziciotipus, Iktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, Deleted,Automata,AutomataKKID)
			select top 1 @UjKK,Poziciotipus, Iktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, 0,dbo.msk_tob_getma(),@kkID  from msk_tob_headpozicio where Idkeresesikerelem=@kkID			
	end

END

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_msk_kex_advertlistchangelog_frissites] @AllasID INT	
AS 
BEGIN

		--DECLARE @Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID INT
		--DECLARE @AdvertListID INT
		--DECLARE @WebAdvertsID INT

		DECLARE @Categories varchar(8000)

		DECLARE @Tasks VARCHAR(8000)
		DECLARE @Additional_Info VARCHAR(8000)
		DECLARE @Recruiter_Info VARCHAR(8000)
		DECLARE @Recruiter_ID VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Recruiter_email VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Recruiter_Felvado VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Map_Job VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @CV VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Subsidiary VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Industry VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Hierarchy_Level VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Education_Type VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Education_Field VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Field_Of_Study VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Reference_Number VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Approval_Date VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Number_Of_Positions VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Created DATETIME 
		DECLARE @Deleted TINYINT

		--DECLARE @Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID_log INT 
		--DECLARE @AdvertListID_log INT 
		--DECLARE @WebAdvertsID_log INT 
		DECLARE @AdvertID_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Company_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Title_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Description_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Locations_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Categories_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @CompanyID_log varchar(8000) 
		DECLARE @Department_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Requirements_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Qualities_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Benefits_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Min_Experience_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Min_Education_log VARCHAR(8000)

		DECLARE @Expiraton_Date_log VARCHAR(8000)

		DECLARE @Map_Job_log VARCHAR(8000)

		DECLARE @Industry_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Hierarchy_Level_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Education_Type_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Education_Field_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Field_Of_Study_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Reference_Number_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Approval_Date_log VARCHAR(8000) 
		DECLARE @Number_Of_Positions_log VARCHAR(8000)

		-- @Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID
		--,@AdvertListID

		 @AdvertID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID
		,@Company = c.Name
		,@Title = ah.Targy
		,@Description = ah.Vallalatibemutatkozo
		,@Locations = CONCAT('<LOCATION>', t.Telepules, '</LOCATION>')
		,@Categories = k.SzakteruletID
		,@CompanyID = k.Idceg
		,@Department = k.SzakteruletID
		,@Requirements = ah.Elvarasok
		,@Qualities = ah.Elonytjelent

		,@Min_Education = NULL
		,@Driver_Licence = 'False'

		FROM dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem k 
		LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek ah ON ah.Idkeresesikerelem=k.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID
		LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek t ON t.Msk_tob_telepulesekID=k.MunkavegzeshelyeID

		LEFT JOIN dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok ff ON ff.Msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifokID=k.FoglalkoztatasifokID
		LEFT JOIN dbo.People AS p ON k.Idtoborzo1 = p.PeopleID
		WHERE ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID=@AllasID
		
		--Legutolsó advertlog id kinyerése 
		DECLARE @MaxAdvertlistchangelogID INT
		SET @MaxAdvertlistchangelogID = (SELECT MAX(Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID) FROM dbo.msk_kex_advertlistchangelog WHERE AdvertID=@AdvertID)

		SELECT
		--,@Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID_log INT

		--,@WebAdvertsID_log INT 
		 @AdvertID_log = AdvertID

		,@Expiraton_Date_log = Expiraton_Date

		,@Additional_Info_log = Additional_Info
		,@Recruiter_Info_log = Recruiter_Info
		,@Recruiter_id_log = Recruiter_ID
		,@Recruiter_Email_log = Recruiter_Email
		,@Recruiter_Felvado_log = Recruiter_Felvado
		,@Map_Job_log = Map_Job
		,@CV_log = CV
		,@Subsidiary_log = Subsidiary
		,@Industry_log = Industry
		,@Hierarchy_Level_log = Hierarchy_Level
		,@Education_Type_log = Education_Type
		,@Education_Field_log = Education_Field
		,@Field_Of_Study_log = Field_Of_Study
		,@Reference_Number_log = Reference_Number
		,@Approval_Date_log = Approval_Date
		,@Number_Of_Positions_log = Number_Of_Positions
		FROM dbo.msk_kex_advertlistchangelog
		WHERE Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID = @MaxAdvertlistchangelogID

		--"Történt-e módosítás?" vizsgálat
		IF
			ISNULL(@Title,'') <> ISNULL(@Title_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Description,'') <> ISNULL(@Description_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Categories,'') <> ISNULL(@Categories_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@CompanyID ,'') <> ISNULL(@CompanyID_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Department,'') <> ISNULL(@Department_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Requirements,'') <> ISNULL(@Requirements_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Qualities,'') <> ISNULL(@Qualities_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Benefits,'') <> ISNULL(@Benefits_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Link,'') <> ISNULL(@Link_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Expiraton_Date,'') <> ISNULL(@Expiraton_Date_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Contract,'') <> ISNULL(@Contract_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Schedule,'') <> ISNULL(@Schedule_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Vacancy_NR,'') <> ISNULL(@Vacancy_NR_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Work_Location,'') <> ISNULL(@Work_Location_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Tasks,'') <> ISNULL(@Tasks_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Additional_Info,'') <> ISNULL(@Additional_Info_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Recruiter_Info,'') <> ISNULL(@Recruiter_Info_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Recruiter_ID,'') <> ISNULL(@Recruiter_id_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Recruiter_email,'') <> ISNULL(@Recruiter_Email_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Recruiter_Felvado,'') <> ISNULL(@Recruiter_Felvado_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Map_Job,'') <> ISNULL(@Map_Job_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@CV,'') <> ISNULL(@CV_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Industry,'') <> ISNULL(@Industry_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Hierarchy_Level,'') <> ISNULL(@Hierarchy_Level_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Education_Type,'') <> ISNULL(@Education_Type_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Education_Field,'') <> ISNULL(@Education_Field_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Field_Of_Study,'') <> ISNULL(@Field_Of_Study_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Reference_Number,'') <> ISNULL(@Reference_Number_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Approval_Date,'') <> ISNULL(@Approval_Date_log,'') OR
			ISNULL(@Number_Of_Positions,'') <> ISNULL(@Number_Of_Positions_log,'')
			OR NOT EXISTS (SELECT * FROM dbo.msk_kex_advertlistchangelog WHERE AdvertID=@AdvertID)
		BEGIN
			INSERT INTO dbo.msk_kex_advertlistchangelog (AdvertListID, Deleted) VALUES (0, 0)

			DECLARE @Uj_msk_kex_advertlistchangelogID INT
			SET @Uj_msk_kex_advertlistchangelogID = SCOPE_IDENTITY()

			UPDATE dbo.msk_kex_advertlistchangelog SET
				AdvertListID = (@Uj_msk_kex_advertlistchangelogID + 4000000),
				AdvertID = @AdvertID,
				Company = @Company,
				Title = @Title,
				Description = @Description,
				Locations = @Locations,
				Categories = @Categories,
				CompanyID = @CompanyID,
				Department = @Department,
				Requirements = @Requirements,
				Qualities = @Qualities,
				Benefits = @Benefits,
				Min_Experience = @Min_Experience,
				Min_Education = @Min_Education,
				Driver_Licence = @Driver_Licence,
				Link = @Link,
				Activation_Date = @Activation_Date,
				Expiraton_Date = @Expiraton_Date,
				Contract = @Contract,
				Schedule = @Schedule,
				Company_Name = @Company_Name,
				Email = @Email,
				Phone = @Phone,
				Vacancy_NR = @Vacancy_NR,
				Work_Location = @Work_Location,
				Hide_Company = @Hide_Company,
				Schow_Apply_Button = @Schow_Apply_Button,
				Custom_Template_ID = @Custom_Template_ID,
				Tasks = @Tasks,
				Additional_Info = @Additional_Info,
				Recruiter_Info = @Recruiter_Info,
				Recruiter_ID = @Recruiter_ID,
				Recruiter_Email = @Recruiter_email,
				Recruiter_Felvado = @Recruiter_Felvado,
				Map_Job = @Map_Job,
				CV = @CV,
				Subsidiary = @Subsidiary,
				Industry = @Industry,
				Hierarchy_Level = @Hierarchy_Level,
				Education_Type = @Education_Type,
				Education_Field = @Education_Field,
				Field_Of_Study = @Field_Of_Study,
				Reference_Number = @Reference_Number,
				Approval_Date = @Approval_Date,
				Number_Of_Positions = @Number_Of_Positions,
				Created = GETDATE()
			WHERE Msk_Kex_AdvertlistchangelogID = @Uj_msk_kex_advertlistchangelogID
		END

END

--TOB Engedélyezõ csoport hozzáadása
IF NOT EXISTS(SELECT TOP 1 1 FROM dbo.People WHERE TechnicalName='Group_TOBENG' AND Deleted=0)
BEGIN
 INSERT INTO dbo.People (CompanyID,Name,IsGroup,CreatedbyID,Active,TechnicalName)
	VALUES ( 0, 'TOB Engedélyezõ', 1, 1, 1, 'Group_TOBENG')
END
ELSE
BEGIN
	PRINT 'TOB Egedélyezõ szerepkör már létezik'
END

	DECLARE @AdvertLZCursor CURSOR
	DECLARE @AllasID INT

		BEGIN
			SET @AdvertLZCursor = CURSOR FOR
			SELECT Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek WHERE Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID >= 60000000

				OPEN @AdvertLZCursor 
				FETCH NEXT FROM @AdvertLZCursor 
				INTO @AllasID

				WHILE @@FETCH_STATUS = 0
				BEGIN

				  EXEC [dbo].[msk_tob_msk_kex_advertlistchangelog_frissites] @AllasID

				  FETCH NEXT FROM @AdvertLZCursor
				  INTO @AllasID
				END; 

				CLOSE @AdvertLZCursor;
				DEALLOCATE @AdvertLZCursor;
			END;
PRINT 'TOB POSTD Ended'

-- =============================================
-- Author:		Horváth Gábor
-- Create date: 2022.05.16
-- Description:	Selenium teszt
-- =============================================
CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_selenium] @mode varchar(10), @servername varchar(100)
AS
BEGIN 
	declare @s varchar(50) = concat('Selenium ',@mode)
	declare @s2 varchar(200)
	exec dbo.msk_kki_log_insert @s,''

	if @servername='localhost/effector68' begin

		delete from [dbo].[msk_kex_interju]
		delete from [dbo].[msk_kex_jelentkezok]
		delete from [dbo].[msk_kex_allasajanlatok]
		delete from msk_tob_allashirdetesek
		delete from dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem

		set @s2 = concat('Táblák teszthez kiürítve: ' , @servername)
		exec dbo.msk_kki_log_insert @s,@s2
	end

END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_setma.sql =====

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_setma]
	@dt datetime 
AS
begin
	IF not EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup WHERE code = 'TOB_GETMA')
		INSERT INTO dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup (Codevalue,CODE,DELETED) VALUES ('','TOB_GETMA',0)
	if @dt is null
		UPDATE dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup SET Deleted=1 WHERE CODE='TOB_GETMA'
	else
		UPDATE dbo.FSYS_ApplicationSetup SET Deleted=0, CodeValue=FORMAT (@dt, 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss') WHERE CODE='TOB_GETMA'
	RETURN 0
end

/* .........................................
TEST 
Az alábbi részlet beállítja konkrét dátumra majd vissza az aktuálisra a dátumot.
Az idõpont részlet mindig a napi aktuális idõt mutatja csak a dátum áll át

EXEC dbo.msk_tob_setma '2022-12-12 12:12:00'
SELECT dbo.msk_tob_getma()
EXEC dbo.msk_tob_setma null
SELECT dbo.msk_tob_getma()

*/

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msk_tob_STA_dll_select.sql =====


CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_STA_DLL_select]	
AS
BEGIN
select (
select PID as "@ID",
ISNULL(case when ltrim(PCOMPANY)='' then '-' else PCOMPANY END,'') as company,
ISNULL(PTITLE,'') as title, 
ISNULL(PDESCRIPTION,'') as description, 
ISNULL(plocation,'') as 'locations/location', 
ISNULL(pcategory,'') as 'categories/category',
ISNULL(PcompanyID,'') as companyID, 
ISNULL(pdepartment,'') as department, 
ISNULL(prequirements,'') as requirements, 
ISNULL(pqualities,'') as qualities, 
ISNULL(pbenefits,'') as benefits, 
ISNULL(pminexperience,'') as min_experience, 
ISNULL(pmineducation,'') as min_education, 
ISNULL(pdriverlicence,'') as driver_license,
ISNULL(plink,'') as link, 
ISNULL(pactivationdate,'') as activation_date, 
ISNULL(pexpirationdate,'') as expiration_date, 
ISNULL(pcontract,'') as contract, 
ISNULL(pschedule,'') as schedule, 
ISNULL(pcompanyname,'') as company_name, 
ISNULL(pemail,'') as email, 
ISNULL(pphone,'') as phone, 
ISNULL(PVACANCYNUMBER,'') as vacancy_nr, 
ISNULL(pworklocation,'') as work_location, 
'false' as hide_company, 
'false' as show_apply_button, 
ISNULL(pcustomtemplateID,'') as custom_template_ID, 
ISNULL(ptasks,'') as tasks, 
ISNULL(padditionalinfo,'') as additional_info, 
ISNULL(precruiterinfo,'') as recruiter_info, 
ISNULL(pfenykepurl,'') as fenykepurl,
ISNULL(pvideourl,'') as videourl,
ISNULL(pproperties,'') as properties
from msk_tob_STA /* where padditionalinfo is not null and padditionalinfo<>'' */
for xml path('advert'), root('WebAdverts')
) as xml
end

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msk_tob_STA_item] 
@ID int
AS
BEGIN
	update msk_tob_allashirdetesek set StatuszSTA=1 where Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = @ID


	insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('STA Interfész ITEM OK',@ID,getdate())
	select 'True'
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Stored Procedures\msp_tob_getIktatoszam.sql =====

/*
    Created by: Gabor Horvath 2024.01.29 
    TOB Iktatószám generátor. 
    Visszad: Utoljára generált iktatószám 
    
Mûködés:

Ellenõrzi, hogy az Idkeresesikerelem már létezik-e a msk_tob_headpozicio táblában. Ha igen, meghatározza a Poziciotipus-t 
és kiválasztja a már meglévõ iktatószám vállalatnevét. Ha nem, akkor beállít egy jelzõt (@ujhead) az új head rekord létrehozására.
Ellenõrzi, hogy az Idkeresesikerelem már létezik-e a msk_tob_pozicio táblában. Ha nem, akkor generál egy új sorszámot. 
Ha igen, akkor csak növeli az alszámot.
Beszúr rekordokat az msk_tob_pozicio táblába a @tanfolyamos és @mennyiseg paraméterek alapján:
- Ha a rekord tanfolyamos (@tanfolyamos = 1), akkor @mennyiseg darabszámú rekordot szúr be, minden egyes rekordhoz növelve az alszámot.
- Ha a rekord nem tanfolyamos (@tanfolyamos = 0), akkor csak egy rekordot szúr be, figyelmen kívül hagyva a @mennyiseg paraméter értékét.
Ha szükséges, létrehoz egy új rekordot a msk_tob_headpozicio táblában, vagy frissíti a meglévõ rekord iktatószámát.
    
*/
CREATE PROCEDURE dbo.msp_tob_getIktatoszam 
    @Idkeresesikerelem INT, 
    @VallalatRovidNeve VARCHAR(50), 
    @tanfolyamos BIT, 
    @mennyiseg INT,
    @datum date,
    @PozicioInfo varchar(50)
AS
BEGIN
    SET NOCOUNT ON;

    DECLARE @Ev INT = YEAR(dbo.msk_tob_getma());
    DECLARE @UjIktatoszam VARCHAR(100);
    DECLARE @MaxSorszam INT;
    DECLARE @Alszam INT;
    DECLARE @PozicioTipus INT;
    DECLARE @IsVanHeadPozicio BIT;
    DECLARE @IsVanPozicio BIT;
    DECLARE @LegutolsoIktatoszam VARCHAR(100);
	DECLARE @AktualisVallalatNeve VARCHAR(50);
	DECLARE @ujhead INT =0
    DECLARE @HeadIktatoszam VARCHAR(100);
    DECLARE @ElsodlegesEngedelyezesiDatum DATE;

insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('msp_tob_getIktatoszam1',concat(isnull(@Idkeresesikerelem,'-'),'|',isnull(@VallalatRovidNeve,'-'),'|',isnull(@tanfolyamos,'-'),'|',isnull(@mennyiseg,'-'),'|',isnull(cast(@datum as varchar(20)),'-'),'|',isnull(@PozicioInfo,'-')),getdate())

    -- Ellenõrzés, hogy létezik-e már a keresési kérelem
    SELECT @IsVanHeadPozicio             = CASE WHEN COUNT(*) > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END
		  ,@LegutolsoIktatoszam          = MAX(Iktatoszam)
          ,@ElsodlegesEngedelyezesiDatum = MIN(Engedelyezesidatum)
    FROM msk_tob_headpozicio
    WHERE ( Idkeresesikerelem = @Idkeresesikerelem ) AND DELETED<2

    -- Ugyanolyan jellegû iktatószám lehet másfelé is ha másolt


    -- @PozicioTipus,@VallalatRovidNeve,@tanfolyamos
    IF @IsVanHeadPozicio = 1
    BEGIN
        SELECT @PozicioTipus = Poziciotipus
        FROM msk_tob_headpozicio
        WHERE ( Idkeresesikerelem = @Idkeresesikerelem or Idkeresesikerelem in (Select distinct AutomataKKID from msk_tob_headpozicio where deleted=0 AND AutomataKKID=@Idkeresesikerelem)) AND DELETED<2		
        SET @VallalatRovidNeve = LEFT(@LegutolsoIktatoszam, CHARINDEX('-', @LegutolsoIktatoszam) - 1);
        SET @tanfolyamos = CASE WHEN @PozicioTipus = 41 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        SET @PozicioTipus = CASE WHEN @tanfolyamos = 1 THEN 41 ELSE 40 END;
		SET @ujhead = 1
    END

    -- Ellenõrzés, hogy van-e már bejegyzés a pozicio táblában
    SELECT @IsVanPozicio = CASE WHEN COUNT(*) > 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END FROM msk_tob_pozicio WHERE Idkeresesikerelem = @Idkeresesikerelem AND DELETED<2    
    SELECT @LegutolsoIktatoszam = MAX(Iktatoszam) FROM msk_tob_pozicio WHERE left(iktatoszam,14)=left(@LegutolsoIktatoszam,14) AND DELETED<2		

insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('msp_tob_getIktatoszam2',concat(isnull(@tanfolyamos,'-'),'|',isnull(@mennyiseg,'-'),'|',isnull(cast(@datum as varchar(20)),'-'),'|',isnull(@PozicioInfo,'-')),getdate())
insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('msp_tob_getIktatoszam3',concat(isnull(@IsVanHeadPozicio,'-'),'|',isnull(@LegutolsoIktatoszam,'-'),'|',isnull(cast(@ElsodlegesEngedelyezesiDatum as varchar(20)),'-'),'|',isnull(@IsVanPozicio,'-')),getdate())

    IF @IsVanPozicio = 0
    BEGIN
        -- Új sorszám generálása az aktuális évvel
        SELECT @MaxSorszam = ISNULL(MAX(CONVERT(INT, SUBSTRING(Iktatoszam, CHARINDEX('-', Iktatoszam) + 1, 4))), 0) + 1
        FROM msk_tob_pozicio
        WHERE Iktatoszam LIKE @VallalatRovidNeve + '-%' AND Iktatoszam LIKE '%/' + CAST(@Ev AS VARCHAR) + '/%' AND DELETED<2;
        SET @Alszam = 1;
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        -- Alszám növelése, de az iktatószám évszámát megtartjuk
        SET @MaxSorszam = CONVERT(INT, SUBSTRING(@LegutolsoIktatoszam, CHARINDEX('-', @LegutolsoIktatoszam) + 1, 4));
        SET @Alszam = CONVERT(INT, RIGHT(@LegutolsoIktatoszam, 3)) + 1;
        SET @Ev = CONVERT(INT, SUBSTRING(@LegutolsoIktatoszam, CHARINDEX('/', @LegutolsoIktatoszam) + 1, 4)); -- Az iktatószám évszámának kinyerése
    END

    SET @UjIktatoszam = @VallalatRovidNeve + '-' + RIGHT('0000' + CAST(@MaxSorszam AS VARCHAR), 4) + '/' + CAST(@Ev AS VARCHAR) + '/' + RIGHT('000' + CAST(@Alszam AS VARCHAR), 3);
	SET @headiktatoszam = @UjIktatoszam
    -- Beszúrás az msk_tob_pozicio táblába
insert into msk_log (name,value,created) values ('msp_tob_getIktatoszam4',concat(isnull(@UjIktatoszam,'-'),'|',isnull(@headiktatoszam,'-'),'|',isnull(@MaxSorszam,'-'),'|',isnull(@Alszam,'-'),'|',isnull(@ujhead,'-')),getdate())

    IF @tanfolyamos = 1
    BEGIN
        if @IsVanPozicio = 1 begin
            SET @datum = ISNULL(@ElsodlegesEngedelyezesiDatum, @datum); 
        end

        if @mennyiseg>0 begin
            if @mennyiseg>99 begin
                set @mennyiseg=99
            end
            DECLARE @i INT = 1;
            WHILE @i <= @mennyiseg
            BEGIN
                INSERT INTO msk_tob_pozicio (Idkeresesikerelem, Iktatoszam, Aliktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, StatuszID, Deleted,PozicioInfo)
                VALUES (@Idkeresesikerelem, @UjIktatoszam, @Alszam, @datum, 32, 0,@PozicioInfo);
			    SET @headiktatoszam = @UjIktatoszam
                SET @Alszam = @Alszam + 1;
                SET @UjIktatoszam = @VallalatRovidNeve + '-' + RIGHT('0000' + CAST(@MaxSorszam AS VARCHAR), 4) + '/' + CAST(@Ev AS VARCHAR) + '/' + RIGHT('000' + CAST(@Alszam AS VARCHAR), 3);
                SET @i = @i + 1;
            END
        end
    END
    ELSE
    BEGIN
        INSERT INTO msk_tob_pozicio (Idkeresesikerelem, Iktatoszam, Aliktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, StatuszID, Deleted,PozicioInfo)
        VALUES (@Idkeresesikerelem, @UjIktatoszam, @Alszam, @datum, 32, 0,@PozicioInfo);
    END

    -- Új rekord a headpozicio táblába
	IF @ujhead=1 BEGIN
        INSERT INTO msk_tob_headpozicio (Idkeresesikerelem, Poziciotipus, Iktatoszam, Engedelyezesidatum, Deleted)
        VALUES (@Idkeresesikerelem, @PozicioTipus, @HeadIktatoszam, @datum, 0);
    END ELSE BEGIN
		UPDATE msk_tob_headpozicio SET Iktatoszam = @HeadIktatoszam WHERE Idkeresesikerelem = @Idkeresesikerelem;
	END

	--SELECT @HeadIktatoszam
END
GO

CREATE PROCEDURE [dbo].[msp_tob_tomeges_portalallashirdetes]
AS 
BEGIN
	SET NOCOUNT ON
	

	SELECT Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID FROM dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek
	WHERE Pubcsoportportal=1 AND Datum_lejarat > GETDATE()

END

-- =============================================
-- Author:		Najdanovszki Krisztián	
-- Create date: 2019.10.03.
-- Description:	Keresési kérelem lezárása false estén törölje a lezárás indoka mezõt
-- =============================================
CREATE TRIGGER keresesikerelem_update
   ON  dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem
   AFTER UPDATE
AS 
BEGIN
	-- SET NOCOUNT ON added to prevent extra result sets from
	-- interfering with SELECT statements.
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	
	UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem SET StatuszID = NULL WHERE Lezaras = 'false'

END
GO

    ON [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem]([SzakteruletID] ASC, [Deleted] ASC);


GO
