-- =============================================
-- Author:		<Author,,Name>
-- Create date: <Create Date,,>
-- Description:	<Description,,>
-- =============================================
CREATE TRIGGER [dbo].[VezetoNullazo]
   ON  [dbo].[msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok]
   AFTER UPDATE, INSERT
AS 
BEGIN
	-- Ha a törölt vezetõ egybe STvezetõ is akkor nulláza az idvezetõt
	SET NOCOUNT ON;
	DECLARE @newAZ int;
	DECLARE @newIdvezeto int;
	DECLARE @newIDKK int;
	DECLARE @newMjgy int;
	DECLARE @newStatuszolovezeto TINYINT;
	DECLARE @newDeleted int;
	DECLARE @MJGYtsz varchar(10);
	SELECT 
	@newAZ= Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID, 
	@newIdvezeto = Idvezeto, 
	@newIDKK = Idkeresesikerelem,
	@newMjgy = Mjgy,
	@newStatuszolovezeto = Statuszolovezeto,
	@newDeleted=Deleted 
	FROM inserted

	IF @newStatuszolovezeto = 1
	BEGIN
	  UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok
	  SET Statuszolovezeto = 0
	  WHERE Idkeresesikerelem = @newIDKK AND NOT idvezeto = @newIdvezeto
	END

	IF @newStatuszolovezeto = 0
	BEGIN
	  UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok
	  SET Statuszolovezeto = 0
	  WHERE Msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetokID=@newAZ
	END

	INSERT dbo.msk_log
	(
	    name,
	    value,
	    created
	)
	VALUES
	(   'statuszoló',           -- name - varchar(100)
	    @newStatuszolovezeto,           -- value - varchar(max)
	    SYSDATETIME() -- created - datetime2(7)
	    )


	IF @newDeleted = 1 
	BEGIN
		-- Ha a törölt vezetõ egybe STvezetõ is akkor nulláza az idvezetõt
--		IF @newMjgy = 9  
--		BEGIN
--			UPDATE msk_kex_allasajanlatok SET idvezeto = NULL  WHERE msk_kex_allasajanlatokID = @newIdallasajanlat AND idvezeto = @newIdvezeto
--		END
		-- Ha a törölt vezetõ munkáltatójogkör gyakorló akkor törli a fiú vezetõket
		IF @newMjgy = 10 
		BEGIN
			SELECT @MJGYtsz = PERNR FROM People WHERE Deleted = 0 AND PeopleID = @newIdvezeto
			UPDATE dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem_vezetok SET Deleted = 1  
			WHERE Idkeresesikerelem = @newIDKK AND Idvezeto in (SELECT PeopleID FROM People WHERE PSTLZ=@MJGYtsz)
		END
	END
END

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Views\msk_tob_CVO.sql =====

CREATE VIEW dbo.msk_tob_CVO
AS
SELECT        dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz.Keresesikerelemstatusz, dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.CVOextID AS PCATEGORY, dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.CVOextID AS PSCHEDULE, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta.CVOextID AS PMINEDUCATION, kk.Pozicioszam AS PVACANCYNUMBER, kk.Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb AS PWORKLOCATION, kk.Cv, kk.Idceg AS PCOMPANYID, ah.Targy AS PTITLE, 
                         ah.Feladatok AS PTASKS, ah.Elvarasok AS PREQUIREMENTS, ah.Elonytjelent AS PQUALITIES, ah.Juttatasok AS PBENEFITS, ah.Fejlecszoveg AS PADDITIONALINFO, 
                         ah.Toborzo_info AS PEMAIL, { fn CONCAT({ fn CONCAT(ah.Toborzonev, ' ') }, ah.Toborzotelefonszam) } AS PRECRUITERINFO, ah.Vallalatibemutatkozo AS PDESCRIPTION, ah.Link AS PLINK, ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID AS PID, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Telepules AS PLOCATION, ah.Datum_publikalas AS PACTIVATIONDATE, dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.Szerzodesfajta AS PCONTRACT, ah.Datum_lejarat AS PEXPIRATIONDATE, 
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company.Name AS PCOMPANYNAME, 0 AS PHIDECOMPANY, 0 AS PSHOWAPPLYBUTTON, dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras.CVOextID AS PCUSTOMTEMPLATEID, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok.Igazgatosagok AS PDEPARTMENT, kk.Deleted, ah.Toborzotelefonszam AS PPHONE, dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID AS Hirdetesstatusz, kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID, 
                         232 AS PMINEXPERIENCE, 0 AS PDRIVERLICENCE, dbo.orn_SZI_Company.Name AS PCOMPANY, ah.FenykepURL AS PFENYKEPURL, ah.VideoURL AS PVIDEOURL, ah.Tulajdonsagok AS PPROPERTIES
FROM            dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk ON dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras.Idceg = kk.Idceg LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company ON kk.Idceg = dbo.orn_SZI_Company.AllasVallalatKod LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet ON kk.SzakteruletID = dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.Msk_tob_szakteruletID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesjelleg ON kk.Kepzes_szakiranyID = dbo.msk_tob_kepzesjelleg.Msk_tob_kepzesjellegID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta ON kk.Kepzes_fajtaID = dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta.Msk_tob_kepzesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok ON kk.FoglalkoztatasifokID = dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.Msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifokID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_munkakoricsoport ON kk.MunkakorcsoportID = dbo.msk_tob_munkakoricsoport.Msk_tob_munkakoricsoportID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek ON kk.MunkavegzeshelyeID = dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Msk_tob_telepulesekID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta ON kk.SzerzodesfajtaID = dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.Msk_tob_szerzodesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS ah LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint ON ah.VegzettsegiszintID = dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint.Msk_tob_vegzettsegiszintID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_LookupList ON ah.StatuszID = dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = ah.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz ON kk.StatuszID = dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatuszID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok ON kk.TeruletiigazgatosagID = dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok.Msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagokID
WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID = 22) AND (ah.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (ah.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (ah.PubCVO = 1)
GO

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Views\msk_tob_portalallashirdetes.sql =====

CREATE VIEW dbo.msk_tob_portalallashirdetes
AS
SELECT        ISNULL(1, '') AS EntitasVerzio, ISNULL(ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID, '') AS id, ISNULL(c.Name, '') AS company, ISNULL(ah.Targy, '') AS title, ISNULL(kk.Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb, ISNULL(t.Telepules, '')) AS location, 
                         ISNULL(szt.CSPextID, '') AS category, ISNULL(kk.Idceg, '') AS companyid, ISNULL(kk.SzervezetiegyesegID, '') AS department, ISNULL(ah.Elvarasok, '') AS requirements, ISNULL(ah.Elonytjelent, '') AS qualities, 
                         ISNULL(ah.Juttatasok, '') AS benefits, ISNULL(0, '') AS minExperience, ISNULL(0, '') AS minEducation, ISNULL(0, '') AS driverLicense, ISNULL(ah.Datum_publikalas, '') AS activationDate, ISNULL(ah.Datum_lejarat, '') 
                         AS expirationDate, ISNULL(szf.Szerzodesfajta, '') AS contract, ISNULL(0, '') AS companyName, ISNULL(0, '') AS email, ISNULL(0, '') AS phone, ISNULL(kk.Pozicioszam, '') AS vacancyNumber, 
                         ISNULL(kk.Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb, ISNULL(t.Telepules, '')) AS workLocation, ISNULL(0, '') AS hideCompany, ISNULL(0, '') AS showApplyButton, ISNULL(ah.Feladatok, '') AS tasks, ISNULL(ah.Tulajdonsagok, '') AS properties, 
                         ISNULL(ah.Fejlecszoveg, '') AS additionalInfo, { fn CONCAT({ fn CONCAT(ISNULL(ah.Toborzonev, ''), ' ') }, ISNULL(ah.Toborzotelefonszam, '')) } AS recruiterInfo, ISNULL(p.PERNR, '') AS recruiterId, ISNULL(p.Email, '') 
                         AS recruiterEmail, ISNULL(ah.VideoURL, '') AS recruiterFelvado, ISNULL(kk.Map_job, '') AS MAPJob, ISNULL(kk.Cv, '') AS Cv, ISNULL(kk.Berlatszik, '') AS BrBerVisible, ISNULL(kk.Berkotelezo, '') AS BrBerMandatory, ISNULL(0, '') 
                         AS subsidiary, ISNULL(ti.CSPextID, '') AS tiCSPextID, ISNULL(ah.FenykepURL, '') AS fieldsOfStudy, ISNULL(kk.Idtoborzo1, '') AS Idtoborzo1, ISNULL(kk.Idtoborzo2, '') AS Idtoborzo2, ISNULL(kk.Engedelyezesidatum, '') 
                         AS Engedelyezesidatum, ISNULL(kk.Iktatoszam, '') AS Iktatoszam, ISNULL(ah.Deleted, '') AS Deleted, ISNULL(ah.Link, '') AS Link, ISNULL(ff.CSPextID, '') AS schedule, ISNULL(mkcs.CSPextID, '') AS mkcsCSPextID, 
                         ISNULL(kf.CSPextID, '') AS kfCSPextID, ISNULL(kj.CSPextID, '') AS kjCSPextID, ISNULL(ti.Igazgatosagok, '') AS industry, ISNULL(mkcs.CSPextID, '') AS hierarchyLeve, ISNULL(kf.CSPextID, '') AS educationType, 
                         ISNULL(kj.Kepzesjelleg, '') AS educationField, ISNULL(vl.CVOextID, '') AS customTemplateId, ISNULL(vl.Leiras, '') AS description
FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk INNER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS ah ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = ah.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company AS c ON kk.Idceg = c.AllasVallalatKod LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras AS vl ON kk.Idceg = vl.Idceg LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok AS ff ON kk.FoglalkoztatasifokID = ff.Msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifokID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok AS ti ON kk.TeruletiigazgatosagID = ti.Msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagokID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta AS kf ON kk.Kepzes_fajtaID = kf.Msk_tob_kepzesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesjelleg AS kj ON kk.Kepzes_szakiranyID = kj.Msk_tob_kepzesjellegID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.People AS p ON kk.Idtoborzo1 = p.PeopleID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_munkakoricsoport AS mkcs ON kk.MunkakorcsoportID = mkcs.Msk_tob_munkakoricsoportID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta AS szf ON kk.SzerzodesfajtaID = szf.Msk_tob_szerzodesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek AS t ON t.Msk_tob_telepulesekID = kk.MunkavegzeshelyeID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet AS szt ON szt.Msk_tob_szakteruletID = kk.SzakteruletID
GO

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Views\msk_tob_STA.sql =====

CREATE VIEW dbo.msk_tob_STA
AS
SELECT        dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz.Keresesikerelemstatusz, dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.CVOextID AS PCATEGORY, dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.CVOextID AS PSCHEDULE, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta.CVOextID AS PMINEDUCATION, kk.Pozicioszam AS PVACANCYNUMBER, kk.Munkavegzeshelyeegyeb AS PWORKLOCATION, kk.Cv, kk.Idceg AS PCOMPANYID, ah.Targy AS PTITLE, 
                         ah.Feladatok AS PTASKS, ah.Elvarasok AS PREQUIREMENTS, ah.Elonytjelent AS PQUALITIES, ah.Juttatasok AS PBENEFITS, ah.Fejlecszoveg AS PADDITIONALINFO, 
                         ah.Toborzo_info AS PEMAIL, { fn CONCAT({ fn CONCAT(ah.Toborzonev, ' ') }, ah.Toborzotelefonszam) } AS PRECRUITERINFO, ah.Vallalatibemutatkozo AS PDESCRIPTION, ah.Link AS PLINK, ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID AS PID, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Telepules AS PLOCATION, ah.Datum_publikalas AS PACTIVATIONDATE, dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.Szerzodesfajta AS PCONTRACT, ah.Datum_lejarat AS PEXPIRATIONDATE, 
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company.Name AS PCOMPANYNAME, 0 AS PHIDECOMPANY, 0 AS PSHOWAPPLYBUTTON, dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras.CVOextID AS PCUSTOMTEMPLATEID, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok.Igazgatosagok AS PDEPARTMENT, kk.Deleted, ah.Toborzotelefonszam AS PPHONE, dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID AS Hirdetesstatusz, kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID, 
                         232 AS PMINEXPERIENCE, 0 AS PDRIVERLICENCE, dbo.orn_SZI_Company.Name AS PCOMPANY, ah.FenykepURL AS PFENYKEPURL, ah.VideoURL AS PVIDEOURL, ah.Tulajdonsagok AS PPROPERTIES
FROM            dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras RIGHT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk ON dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras.Idceg = kk.Idceg LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company ON kk.Idceg = dbo.orn_SZI_Company.AllasVallalatKod LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet ON kk.SzakteruletID = dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.Msk_tob_szakteruletID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesjelleg ON kk.Kepzes_szakiranyID = dbo.msk_tob_kepzesjelleg.Msk_tob_kepzesjellegID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta ON kk.Kepzes_fajtaID = dbo.msk_tob_kepzesfajta.Msk_tob_kepzesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok ON kk.FoglalkoztatasifokID = dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.Msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifokID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_munkakoricsoport ON kk.MunkakorcsoportID = dbo.msk_tob_munkakoricsoport.Msk_tob_munkakoricsoportID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek ON kk.MunkavegzeshelyeID = dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Msk_tob_telepulesekID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta ON kk.SzerzodesfajtaID = dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.Msk_tob_szerzodesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS ah LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint ON ah.VegzettsegiszintID = dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint.Msk_tob_vegzettsegiszintID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_LookupList ON ah.StatuszID = dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = ah.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz ON kk.StatuszID = dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatusz.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemstatuszID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok ON kk.TeruletiigazgatosagID = dbo.msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagok.Msk_tob_teruletiigazgatosagokID
WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (ah.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (ah.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID = 22) AND (ah.PubSTA = 1)
GO
EXECUTE sp_addextendedproperty @name = N'MS_DiagramPaneCount', @value = 3, @level0type = N'SCHEMA', @level0name = N'dbo', @level1type = N'VIEW', @level1name = N'msk_tob_STA';

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Views\msk_tob_STA_OLD_eredeti.sql =====

CREATE VIEW dbo.[msk_tob_STA_OLD_eredeti]
AS
SELECT        ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID AS PITEMID, vl.STAextID AS PREFID, ah.Toborzonev AS PCONTACTNAME, ah.Toborzotelefonszam AS PCONTACTPHONE, ah.Targy AS PTITLE,
                             (SELECT        { fn CONCAT
                                                             ((SELECT        { fn CONCAT
                                                                                              ((SELECT        { fn CONCAT
                                                                                                                               ((SELECT        { fn CONCAT
                                                                                                                                                                ((SELECT        { fn CONCAT
                                                                                                                                                                                                 ((SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Feladatok, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT('   Feladatok: ', aha.Feladatok)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                                                                                                                                                                     FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              dbo.msk_tob_LookupList ON aha.StatuszID = dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID
                                                                                                                                                                                                     WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              AND (dbo.msk_tob_LookupList.LookupListID = 22) AND (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID)),
                                                                                                                                                                                                 (SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Elvarasok, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT('    Elvárások: ', aha.Elvarasok)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                             END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                                                                                                                                                                   FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                                                             dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                                                             dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_6 ON aha.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_6.LookupListID
                                                                                                                                                                                                   WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) AND
                                                                                                                                                                                                                              (msk_tob_LookupList_6.LookupListID = 22) AND (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND 
                                                                                                                                                                                                                             (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID))) } AS Expr1),
                                                                                                                                                                (SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Elonytjelent, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT('    Elõnyt jelent: ', aha.Elonytjelent)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                                                                                                                                  FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                            dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                                                            dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_5 ON aha.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_5.LookupListID
                                                                                                                                                                  WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) AND 
                                                                                                                                                                                            (msk_tob_LookupList_5.LookupListID = 22) AND (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID))) 
                                                                                                                                                            } AS Expr1),
                                                                                                                               (SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Juttatasok, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT('    Juttatások: ', aha.Juttatasok)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                                                                                                 FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                           dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                                                           dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_4 ON aha.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_4.LookupListID
                                                                                                                                 WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) AND 
                                                                                                                                                           (msk_tob_LookupList_4.LookupListID = 22) AND (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID))) } AS Expr1),
                                                                                              (SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Toborzonev, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT('    További információ: ', aha.Toborzonev)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                                                                FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                          dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                                                          dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_3 ON aha.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_3.LookupListID
                                                                                                WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) AND (msk_tob_LookupList_3.LookupListID = 22) 
                                                                                                                          AND (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID))) } AS Expr1),
                                                             (SELECT        CASE WHEN (ISNULL(aha.Toborzotelefonszam, '') <> '') THEN (CONCAT(' ', aha.Toborzotelefonszam)) ELSE (CONCAT('', '')) END AS PDESCRIPTION
                                                               FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                         dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS aha ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = aha.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                                                                                         dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_2 ON aha.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_2.LookupListID
                                                               WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Deleted = 0) AND (aha.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (aha.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (aha.PubSTA = 1) AND (msk_tob_LookupList_2.LookupListID = 22) AND 
                                                                                         (aha.StatuszCSP = 1) AND (aha.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID = ah.Msk_tob_allashirdetesekID))) } AS Expr1) AS PDESCRIPTION, dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.STAextID AS PREGIO, 0 AS PAR, 
                         ah.FenykepURL AS PIMAGE, ah.Link AS PURL, dbo.orn_SZI_Company.Name AS PCEGNEV_SZEKTOR, kk.Munkakor AS PPOZICIO, dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.STAextID AS PORIENTACIO, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Telepules AS PMUNKAVEGZES_HELYE, dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint.Vegzettsegiszint AS PISKOLAI_VEGZETTSEG, ' ' AS PNYELVTUDAS, kk.Lejaratidatum AS PJELENTKEZESI_HATARIDO, 
                         dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.STAextID AS PFOGLALKOZTATAS_MODJA, dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.STAextID AS PMUNKAIDO, 'versenyképes' AS PFIZETESI_SZINT, ' ' AS PSPECIALIS_JELLEG
FROM            dbo.msk_tob_keresesikerelem AS kk LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_allashirdetesek AS ah ON kk.Msk_tob_keresesikerelemID = ah.Idkeresesikerelem LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek ON kk.MunkavegzeshelyeID = dbo.msk_tob_telepulesek.Msk_tob_telepulesekID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet ON kk.SzakteruletID = dbo.msk_tob_szakterulet.Msk_tob_szakteruletID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.orn_SZI_Company ON kk.Idceg = dbo.orn_SZI_Company.AllasVallalatKod LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint ON ah.VegzettsegiszintID = dbo.msk_tob_vegzettsegiszint.Msk_tob_vegzettsegiszintID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok ON kk.FoglalkoztatasifokID = dbo.msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifok.Msk_tob_foglalkoztatasifokID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta ON kk.SzerzodesfajtaID = dbo.msk_tob_szerzodesfajta.Msk_tob_szerzodesfajtaID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_LookupList AS msk_tob_LookupList_1 ON ah.StatuszID = msk_tob_LookupList_1.LookupListID LEFT OUTER JOIN
                         dbo.msk_tob_vallalatleiras AS vl ON kk.Idceg = vl.Idceg
WHERE        (kk.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Deleted = 0) AND (ah.Pubcsoportportal = 1) AND (ah.Datum_lejarat >= GETDATE()) AND (ah.PubSTA = 1) AND (msk_tob_LookupList_1.LookupListID = 22) AND (ah.StatuszCSP = 1)
GO

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Views\msk_tob_szervezetiegyseg.sql =====

CREATE VIEW dbo.msk_tob_szervezetiegyseg
AS
SELECT DISTINCT ORGEH AS Kod, ORGTX AS Nev, BUKRS
FROM            dbo.People
WHERE        (Deleted = 0)
GO

===== FILE: C:\hop2\src\Hrportal-Root\HRPortalDB\dbo\Functions\Max2.sql =====

create function Max2(@val1 int, @val2 int)
returns int
as
begin
  if @val1 > @val2
    return @val1
  return isnull(@val2,@val1)
end
